Axir kan ad am-d-iniɣ tidet.
Axir kan ad akent-d-iniɣ tidet.
Axir kan ad awen-d-iniɣ tidet.
Tamussni-nsen d aɣilifi.
Iban-d win i t-yessnen.
Ulac tirect ur nesεi akerfa.
Yerreẓ ufus n ugelzim.
Ayen yelhan deg tmurt-a yettruḥ.
Axeddim akk i d-yettifriren, teggen-as uguren.
Ahat la thellkeḍ iman-ik s wayagi akk, ḍegger akin!
D axeddim i yettifriren iwumi teggen kra n medden iεekkiṛen.
Teqqar yemma: "Yir awal seg yir xenfuc."
Xdem neɣ qqim, ur tesεiḍ acu i d-tsuliḍ.
Ur stufaɣ ara akk ass-a.
Meṛṛa icettiḍen-inu d yemma i ten-iserden
Mačči akk arrac ḥemmlen tteffaḥ.
Acḥal icbaḥ ujeǧǧig-a.
Taglizit teshel i ulmad.
Wa ad iruḥ, ad d-yuɣal.
Yiwen ad yemmet, wayeḍ ad d-ilal.
Wa yettnadi ɣef talwit.
Wa deg ccwal ideg yettnawal.
Yal yiwen d acu i yessaram.
Yal wa d asirem-is.
Err-as zzeṛb.
Yemma temmut asmi lliɣ d amecṭuḥ.
Ur tesεiḍ d acu ara tagadeḍ, Tom.
Seččayen-k?
Seččayen-kem?
Seččayen-ken?
Seččayen-kent?
Seččayent-k?
Seččayent-kem?
Seččayent-ken?
Seččayent-kent?
Wid iɣellqen tiwwura yeldin.
Ayen riɣ mačči d awal; mi t-id-tenniḍ, yeddem-it waḍu.
Bdiɣ lemmdeɣ tafṛansist asmi sεiɣ 30 yiseggasen deg leεmeṛ-iw.
Lemdeɣ-d amek ara sewwayeɣ ɣur Tom.
Γur Tom i d-lemdeɣ amek ara sewwayeɣ.
Ur iyi-yeεǧib ara amek i d-iεenna Tom.
Ḥefḍeɣ-d amek ara sewwayeɣ ɣur Tom.
Tom iwεed ad d-yefk afus n tallelt.
Tom iwεed ad d-yefk afus n lemεawna.
Tom iwεed ad d-yefk ad iεawen.
Tom yenna-yi-d ad d-lhuɣ yid-k akken ilaq.
Tom yenna-yi-d ad d-lhuɣ yid-m akken ilaq.
Tom yenna-yi-d ad d-lhuɣ yid-kent akken ilaq.
Tom yenna-yi-d ad d-lhuɣ yid-wen akken ilaq.
Acḥal i trebḥeḍ?
Acḥal i trebḥem?
Acḥal i trebḥemt?
